# SparkStreamingLeak

Code that illustrates resource leak related to class loaders and updateStateByKey.
The number of classes loaded steadily increases until failure occurs. 

## UPDATE 
These problems only occur when master is local[*]. 

The problem does not occur when using a local cluster

## UPDATE TWO

The 1.4.0 release resolves the problem.

## Process

Start two sbt instances. 
Run Generator in first to provide source of streaming data.
Run one of the test programs in the other sbt

Monitor the test program using jconsole or jvisualvm

Any program that uses a case class eventually fails (after 3 - 30 hours), when the
number of classes loaded reaches approximately 2 million instances. The total number of classes actually loaded
starts at ~7 000 and grows to approximately 10 000.

A test that uses only native Scala classes does not exhibit this behavior.

The created classes are of the form
```
Loaded sun.reflect.GeneratedSerializationConstructorAccessor125 from __JVM_DefineClass__
```

One run failed with the following exception, which I have not been able to replicate.
